I	Most sources give the recommended reading age for Redwall of around  oftentimes many bookstores simply listed as ages  and up for simplicity Some sources may have recommended age ranges for Redwall as broad as  or  while others a narrower  in the same source Another store has it listed as  Judging by those provided ages Redwall is suitable for people in middle school To sum it up younger Redwall readers are  in between readers are  while older readers are  The age rating may have something to do with both the reading level as the books are written to be readable by a person in thth grade independently  Redwall has the same age range as the Harry Potter books another favourite amongst middle schoolers The difference between Redwall and Harry Potter is the nature of the combat and the genre Redwall being little to no magic in a fictional world Harry Potter being high magic in pockets of fantasy within the real world  As Harry ages the books also progressively becomes darker over time Yet another middle school favourite is Percy Jackson and the Olympians the first installments in the Camp HalfBlood series later followed by The Heroes of Olympus and The Trials of Apollo all for ages  or  The combat is more magical akin to that of Harry Potter Older childrensmiddle grade literature and teenageyoung adult literature have very fuzzy lines and oftentimes many including Redwall Camp HalfBlood and Harry Potter are classified as both most likely due to all dwelling in between these two categories in age While these aforementioned series are more complex mature dark violent and tragic compared to other middle grade novels for ages  they are still written well within the guidelines of middle grade fiction This is also the case for the Alex Rider spy novels although the genre and tone is very different from Redwall I have heard of them since th grade Despite being a kids series Alex Rider is brutal definitely not the story with a happy ending many people would like While the content isnt really the same the Discworld younger readers books are for readers of the same age The Discworld younger readers started with The Amazing Maurice and his Educated Rodents to the Tiffany Aching witch stories Discworld ended with the last Tiffany Aching book The Shepherds Crown Like The Rogue Crew in Redwall The Shepherds Crown is published posthumously   The original Redwall animated series rated TVY is toned down in all aspects and for a younger age than the books  and  years old due to the standards of the network it aired on In my opinion Redwall adaptations should be PGTVV to capture the tone of the books which makes sense  and  is within the recommended reading age and a person doesnt necessarily need to be at that age and older to watch the movieanimated series The purpose of a Redwall adaptation isnt to have it be as kid friendly as possible rather it is to give a sense of familiar nostalgia or feel the books have A typical  year old can also sit through and even enjoy all of the intense scenes speaking from personal experience As for the worst deaths they are given discretion shots and arent lingered on There is also a lack of an actionized TV western animated series No one wants another Rings of Power that is simply a billion dollar fanfiction project that defiles canon Redwall adaptations shouldnt add or retcon anything outside of what is established by Jacques have adaptations of the books with the same details overall  Another grounded low fantasy series I suggest to Redwall readers is called The Rangers Apprentice It is for the exact same age range and the genre as Redwall Like Redwall it is a coming of age story with black and white morality at first anyways it turns to gray and gray morality later on The island the stories are set in Araluen is very similar to Mossflower also vaguely modeled after Great Britain These two book series actually have mutual overlapping readers for being very similar in heroes villains the sense of adventure and the values of friendship The author John Flanagan wrote the original draft to read to his then  year old son the same way Brian Jacques wrote the first Redwall manuscript to read to blind children The Rangers Apprentice also conveys the same message that despite being young and initially unskilled the heroes can achieve their goals with determination In terms of tone reading age plot and source material it is among the closest works of fantasy literature to a Redwall with humans not quite though there are still some fundamental differences There is a sister series called Brotherband Chronicles taking place in the same setting Like Redwall and A Song of Ice and Fire The Rangers ApprenticeBrotherband Chronicles has medieval Europe as the source material for the characters and factions There is also love for food although the food description as expected is far less detailed The food in the series is based on those in medieval Europe oftentimes the foods focused on the most are the pies There is very little magic which is largely unknown and doesnt play an important role in the story with it being largely ambiguous In this case it is more like Redwall as the magic in Game of Thrones is less ambiguous and simply uncommon The villains also have shared traits such as cynicism which many in Redwall and Game of Thrones possess the topic of slavery is also an aspect in the plot It is because of Redwall I found out about this series and many bookstores actually suggest The Rangers ApprenticeBrotherband Chronicles to Redwall readers and the other way around Redwall reading age book category classification and comparison to other popular book series for the same age Ideal movietelevision ratings Another book series I suggest to Redwall readers

I	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased sheigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  domit persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be trying to release at least one a week starting in the new year Acheaa Dream of Divine Scams  Part I

scene that is so prevalent around the United States Born in New York but growing up in Riverdale Georgia Waka Flocka set the underground trap world ablaze with his hit single O Lets Do It in  It wasnt until  with the release of the  club banger Hard in the Paint that mainstream audiences began to notice Waka  more single followed in late  No Hands feat Roscoe Dash and Wale creating an unprecedented buzz for the underground trap artist who was being  groomed and repped by non other than the legends himself Gucci Mane Waka Flocka proceeds to drop in October of  one of the greatest debuts for a hiphop artist of the new decade and in my opinion a certified classic in modern day hiphop Flockaveli almost entirely produced by Lex Luger becomes a staple and blueprint in the modern day trap scene targets such as the Yonko doffy etc And a group tasked with defending the celestial dragons And a group tasked with bolstering technology and military weaponry  SWORD  marines  AEGIS  cipher pol  SSG  science    Vegapunk is the leader of the SSG whilst sentomaru is the captain of the SSG So this group has a captain and a leader The group is focused around science and the man with greatest talent for science and mind for science in the world leads the group which make sense Him and the other most talented scientists in the navy are in this group Vegpunk excels in science more than any other scientist The mental feats of vegapunk are unrivaled no scientist in the marines has created as many things as vegapunk  Now my headcanon on SWORD based on the SSG which is supported by evidence in the story    Garp is the leader of SWORD and we have a captain of SWORD revealed in Drake This group also has a captain and a leader This group is focused around combat and the man with the greatest excels in both combat and strategy he is highly intelligent while garp is not and like luffy is very dense and slow to understand things He has become wise with timeage this doesnt necessarily mean he is smart  Anyway garp is heralded as the greatest marine which means that garps combat ability is minimum equal to sengokus combat ability  strategic ability Roger wanted garp or sengoku he did not marines and he very likely has a blueprint for an ultimate marine he is trying to create   MARINES  Why garp isnt the ultimate marine Being a marine isnt just about combat it has an incredible mental aspect to it which garp is one of the least capable at Strategy Weaponry Psychological warfare  Garps has no talent for using strategy that is why he has one strategy  v the boss and end it but because of how natrually strong garp is this always works for him and is the only strategy he needs  Reference to garps low intelligence even by luffy and others Nami isnt stupid and neither is chopper their assesment is credible  Garp has no talent for armamentweaponry that is why he has one weapon his fists but because of how naturally strong garp is this always works for him and is the this will be GLS In the UK this will be ParcelForce or EVRI formerly known as Hermes usually in times of industrial action RMAs in Europe are by DHL  In Komodo regions we arent sure yet It will almost certainly be a large local courier service Regardless of who ships it you will receive a tracking number to follow your Decks progress  xB  Update for December  via Valve   xB  Starting December st th  xB  Were happy to announce that Steam Decks will start shipping in Japan  South Korea Hong Kong and Taiwan on December th via Komodo our  official Steam Deck distributor in these regions  Customers in these regions can reserve the Steam Deck here steamdeckkomodojp  xB  Source   xB  Im stuck on Shipping Soon help  xB  Its normal for your order to stay on Shipping Soon for several days We usually see Steam Decks delivered within  working days after placing the order A business day is considered MonFri  xB  If it has been longer than  working days and its still on Shipping Soon you should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update in which case you should contact Steam Support  xB  My tracking says preadvice  awaiting parcel help  xB  This is a normal step in the process this means your parcel is somewhere between Valves warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do FedExGLSParcelForce deliver on Sundays  xB  FedEx delivers to  of the US population on a SundaySundaySunday  xB  In Europe as with most delivery companies GLS  ParcelForce does not typically deliver on a Sunday They may do so in times of peak demand around Christmas but outside of this its unlikely  xB  Both FedEx and GLS do deliver on Saturdays though  xB  UK My parcel is stuck in customs what do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for I	Please discuss anything relating to FedEx GLS or ParcelForce here Anything from your experience positive or negative questions regarding delivery wait times or delivery issues and delivery damage images all belong in this megathread  xB  This decision was made on polling our community  xB  Frequently Asked Questions  xB  Who will ship my Steam Deck  xB  In North America USCA this will be FedEx RMAs are also processed by FedEx  xB  In Europe this will be GLS In the UK this will be ParcelForce or EVRI formerly known as Hermes usually in times of industrial action RMAs in Europe are by DHL  xB  In Komodo regions  we arent sure yet It will almost certainly be a large local courier service  xB  Regardless of who ships it you will receive a tracking number to follow your Decks progress  xB  Im stuck on Shipping Soon help  xB  Its normal for your order to stay on Shipping Soon for several days We usually see Steam Decks delivered within  working days after placing the order A business day is considered MonFri  xB  If it has been longer than  working days and its still on Shipping Soon you should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update in which case you should contact Steam Support  xB  My tracking says preadvice  awaiting parcel help  xB  This is a normal step in the process this means your parcel is somewhere between Valves warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do FedExGLSParcelForce deliver on Sundays  xB  FedEx delivers to  of the US population on a SundaySundaySunday  xB  In Europe as with most delivery companies GLS  ParcelForce does not typically deliver on a Sunday They may do so in times of peak demand around Christmas but outside of this its unlikely  xB  Both FedEx and GLS do deliver on Saturdays though  xB  UK My parcel is stuck in customs what do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for customs checks Depending on several events outside of the control of GLSParcelForce there are many different reasons why this could take a long period of time  xB  My Steam Deck is delayed Im annoyed  xB  Sorry to hear that your Steam Deck has been delayed Unfortunately as with any delivery service its possible for issues and delays to occur during the delivery process  xB  So long as your shipping provider is giving you frequent updates and has not elapsed more than  working days without an update hang tight  xB  If you havent received an update in over  working days MonFri please contact Steam Support  xB  My Steam Deck is brokenstolenlost from delivery help  xB  You should I	The first layer of frost had arrived that morning at Camp HalfBlood but the day despite being cold was quiet Sword fighting was ongoing there were some who were riding horses and pegasi over by the canoe lake and as per usual someone was trying not to get lavad on the climbing wall It was a strangely normal day  normal days never happened in this small area of New York state  Dionysus and Chiron had been playing Pinochle for almost two and a half hours this was the tensest and most lively game between the two in over a decade with it seeming to command the full attention of the god and the immortal centaur It was very rare to see such a competitive edge between the two of them This therefore explained why neither of those two noticed the radio flaring to life and the message trying to cut through the static   Ariadne had picked up the radio and was examining it carefully trying to find a way to turn it off there was a curiosity about mortals and their inventions since she had ascended to divinity herself She had just located the off switch when she heard a few words manage to break through the crackled interference she frowned and looked over to where her husband and Chiron were playing and sighed  Both of you listen to this Ariadne instructed as she placed down the radio over the pile of cards that were already on the table which caught the attention of the two of them At first Dionysus looked indigently at his wife for disrupting the game but soon changed his mind as he heard some of the words come through the radio Chiron who hadnt struggled as much to hear the words coming through the radio only sighed  Yo like our part bus has br out of dracma Near bany in NY Chiron dude d some heroes for us  Whilst the message was a garbled mess the three sat around the pinochle table and had heard enough to get the gist of the message The Party Ponies needed help and were calling for help from Camp HalfBlood and the heroes that resided there  Dionysus looked up at Chiron his eyebrow raised in an unasked question but it was Ariadne who answered for the centaur Well we were already looking for allies and this seems perfect We send a quest to aid the Party Ponies and in return they pledge to help the Camp in return She smiled as she looked at Chiron who was already starting to move his fake wheelchair as if he had expected one day something like this would happen  I will send them an iris message and inform them that help is on the way I will also see if they cant be more helpful instead of just sending us broken words Chiron said sighing already imagining the headache that would inevitably come should the Party Ponies come to camp with their music blaring out  Dionysus finally spoke folding his arms in a slight huff that one of the best games of pinochle since he had been stuck with the mortals had been ruined Fine so well help the dancing horses More allies yes yes But not many can withstand their parties they have done some of the most exquisite in all of history How can any of these lot stand up to that Theyd be drunk within an hour and likely get themselves killed Dionysus comments were hardly surprising however he did earn a slap on the arm from his wife for them  I already have some questers in mind some of the older ones who are still not sure of themselves Chiron added as he scribbled down three names on a piece of paper and passed it over to Dionysus who scanned it and nodded in agreement  Those three would do                              It was a little after lunchtime did an announcement go out over the whole of camp disrupting all of the activities currently underway one of those riding a pegasus did end up falling into the canoe lake with an almighty splash  Pax Macblaster Andrew Feybolds and Loopy Heights  come to the Big House straight away  The message was curt and direct although not rude in tone but once again Dionysus was clearly making sure to get the names wrong What wasnt clear however to the whole of camp is what the God of Wine and Parties wanted with the sons of Zeus and Eros and the daughter of Hermes Seasons of Change  The Greatest Party Ever

I	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased sheigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  domit persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be I	Please discuss anything relating to FedEx GLS or ParcelForce here Anything from your experience positive or negative questions regarding delivery wait times or delivery issues and delivery damage images all belong in this megathread  xB   Frequently Asked Questions  xB  Who will ship my Steam Deck  xB  In North America USCA this will be FedEx RMAs are also processed by FedEx  xB  In Europe this will be GLS In the UK this will be ParcelForce or EVRI formerly known as Hermes usually in times of industrial action RMAs in Europe are by DHL  In Komodo regions we arent sure yet It will almost certainly be a large local courier service Regardless of who ships it you will receive a tracking number to follow your Decks progress  xB  Update for December  via Valve   xB  Starting December st customers in Japan South Korea Hong Kong and  Taiwan who have already reserved their Steam Deck will receive email  confirmations to finalize their orders These orders will start shipping  on December th  xB  Were happy to announce that Steam Decks will start shipping in Japan  South Korea Hong Kong and Taiwan on December th via Komodo our  official Steam Deck distributor in these regions  Customers in these regions can reserve the Steam Deck here steamdeckkomodojp  xB  Source   xB  Im stuck on Shipping Soon help  xB  Its normal for your order to stay on Shipping Soon for several days We usually see Steam Decks delivered within  working days after placing the order A business day is considered MonFri  xB  If it has been longer than  working days and its still on Shipping Soon you should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update in which case you should contact Steam Support  xB  My tracking says preadvice  awaiting parcel help  xB  This is a normal step in the process this means your parcel is somewhere between Valves warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do FedExGLSParcelForce deliver on Sundays  xB  FedEx delivers to  of the US population on a SundaySundaySunday  xB  In Europe as with most delivery companies GLS  ParcelForce does not typically deliver on a Sunday They may do so in times of peak demand around Christmas but outside of this its unlikely  xB  Both FedEx and GLS do deliver on Saturdays though  xB  UK My parcel is stuck in customs what do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for customs checks Depending on several events outside of the control of GLSParcelForce there are many different reasons why this could take a long period of time  xB  My Steam Deck is delayed Im annoyed  xB  Sorry to hear that your Steam Deck has been delayed Unfortunately as with any delivery service its possible for issues and delays to occur during the delivery process  xB  So long as your shipping provider is giving you frequent updates and has not elapsed more than  working days without an update hang tight  xB  If you havent received an update in over  working days MonFri please contact Steam Support  xB  My Steam Deck is brokenstolenlost from delivery help  xB  You should contact Steam Support as soon as possible so that a replacement can be arranged  xB  xB   Shipping Megathread January

I	Runner Up Read The Lightning Thief Percy Jackson  The Olympians by Rick Riordan Ch  I Accidentally Vaporize My Maths Teacher through Ch  We Capture a Flag Discussion  Look I didnt want to be a halfblood If youre reading this because you think you might be one my advice is close this book right now  Percy Jackson Rick Riordan  Hello readers Welcome to the first discussion of The Lightning Thief Book  of the Percy Jackson  The Olympians series by Rick Riordan We will be discussing Chapters  I Accidentally Vaporize My Math Teacher through Chapter  We Capture a Flag Feel free to respond to any of the discussion questions below or all of them  A word about spoilers  Percy Jackson is an extremely popular brand with movies books and a TV show Keep in mind that not everyone has watched or read any of these items This book may be the first time a person learns about it Please keep rbookclubs rules on spoilers and the consequences for posting spoilers in mind  Everyone has a different perception of what is a spoiler so here are a few examples of what would be spoilers   Just wait till you see what happens next   This wont be the last time you meet this character   Your prediction is correctincorrect   You will look back at this theory   Here is an Easter Egg    You dont know enough to answer that question yet   How do you firsttimereaders feel about this detail that was intentionally not emphasized by the author  If youre unsure its best to err on the side of caution and use spoiler tags  To indicate a spoiler enclose the relevant text with the   and   characters there is no space inbetween Halfblood camp can be fundepends on who  For any type of comment or idea that may be a part of Percy Jackson just use proper spoiler labels for example In The Sea of Monsters then describe the connection between books Please be mindful when posting  Also when posting a spoiler tag please type what section the spoiler would be from  In chapter  rose said  If you see something that you consider to be a spoiler you can report it It will be removed and the mods will look into it To do so hit the report button click on breaks rbookclub rules next spoilers must be tagged and finally submit  Lets get to it Here are the chapter summaries  Chapter Summaries  Chapter  I Accidentally Vaporize My Maths Teacher  We begin the story with a warning from the title character Percy Jackson He urges us to close the book immediately Percy Jackson is a  year old boy who attends Yancy Academy a private school for troubled kids His life changes dramatically during a field trip to the Metropolitan Museum of Art Previous field trips did not go well for Percy at his previous schools accidents having occurred on every trip On this trip two chaperones led the group of students Mr Brunner the Latin teacher and Percys favorite and Mrs Dodds the math teacher Percys only friend Grover is on the trip as well   After a disagreement with his school bully cy Bobofit at the water fountain Percy is falsely accused of pushing her when she suddenly finds herself soaked in the ankle deep water Mrs Dodds leads Percy away from the group demanding a confession from him as she transforms into a horrid creature with bat wings and yellow fangs Mr Brunner suddenly appears and tosses Percy a ballpoint pen that turns into a bronze sword Percy swings the sword as the monster lunges at him and it turns to dust Dazed by this experience Percy finds that when he returns to the group no one remembers Mrs Dodds   Chapter  Three Old Ladies Knit the Socks of Death  No one recalls that Mrs Dodds was ever at the school or even existed which convinces Percy something else is going on Frustrated that hes the only one that seems to know Percy continues to fight with cy neglect his grades and even disrespect a teacher which gets Percy expelled from Yancey Academy Percy decides the only final he will study for is Mr Brunners Latin final and he goes to Mr Brunners office for help Percy overhears a conversation between Mr Brunner and Grover about Percy and the incident with Mrs Dodds They talk about magical mist making all of the students and teachers forget Mrs Dodds and Grover explains how Percy may be the only one who can save them before the Summer Solstice  After the school year ends Percy confronts Grover on the bus about his conversation with Mr Brunner Grover reveals his role as Percys protector The bus breaks down and as they step off the bus Grover and Percy see three old women knitting huge socks and staring at Percy As Grover makes Percy promise to walk to Percys house together one of the old women cuts a string off the socks with a pair of large shears Grover reveals thanks to Percys prodding that the cut signifies that someones going to die  Chapter  Grover Unexpectedly Loses His Trousers  After the bus stops at the terminal Percy ditches Grover and walks home on his own Before readers enter the apartment Percy describes his mother Sally Jackson the best person Percy knows Shes had some unfortunate things happen in her life though she met Percys father which was the high point though he left on an ocean voyage before Percy was born Sally later married Gabe known as Smelly Gabe by Percy He is a world class jerk immediately to Percy as he goes into the apartment His Mom comes home from her job at the candy store and talks to Percy about his day school etc as Percy eats candy brought home   Sally tells Percy that theyre going to Montauk Beach where shed met Percys father Gabe warns Percy as they leave not to scratch Gabes car and demands bean dip While at the beach Sally tells Percy about his father and Percy learns his father wanted to send Percy to a special camp That night as a hurricane thunders outside a knock on the door wakes Percy and Sally Grover is at the door saying he has been searching for Percy all night Sally is unfazed by Grovers presence and demands that Percy tells her everything that happened at the museum Percy explains and they run to the call Percy realizing that Grover has hooves for feet  Chapter  My Mom Teaches Me Bullfighting  While driving away from the storm Percy sees a large creature following them in the distance He questions how Grover and Sally seem so familiar and what kind of animal Grover is Grover explains that he is Percys protector and a satyr but the less he knows the less monsters he attracts Based on Percys encounter with the three old women who Percy is told were The Fates Sally drives them to the camp Percys father wanted him to go to The car suddenly swerves into a ditch which injures Grover though he demands food Sally encourages Percy to go get help but running past a large Christmas treelike tree marking the boundary line of the camp but he refuses to leave without her or Grover as the creature is gaining on them   Sally and Percy finally manage to get Grover out of the car and head for the boundary Percy sees that the monster is half man half bull which prompts him to name the creature Minotaur but his mom cautions him against it saying names have power She advises him to jump to the side if the creature attacks as bulls cannot change directions suddenly Percy does that as the bull charges which angers it The Minotaur grabbed Percys mother by the neck and she disappeared in a golden light Percy is furious which prompts him to attack the monster tearing off one of its horns and stabbing it in the ribs The creature bursts into dust and Percy drags Grover to safety collapsing on the porch of a farmhouse where a girl calls him the one  Chapter  I Play Pinochle with a Horse  Percy wakes up and passes out over and over being nursed back to health with some pudding tasting like buttered popcorn and the girl calling him the one last night feeding it to him and questioning him Percy wakes up to beautiful views of the camp unlike anything hed ever seen before Still mourning for his mother Percy reflects on the fight last night Grover shows up apologizing for Percys mothers death and failing his role as a keeper Percy does not blame Grover and they leave for the main part of Camp Half Blood Percy meets Mr D the reluctant camp director Chiron who Percy knew as Mr Brunner and Annabeth a Daughter of Athena who nursed him back to health  Percy joins Chiron Mr D and Grover in a game of Pinochle While playing the game they discuss the presence of Greek gods in the world revealing that Mr D is one himself Dionysus the god of wine put in charge of the camp as a punishment from his father Zeus Mr D and Grover leave so Percy and Chiron can talk privately Chiron and Percy discuss more about Mount Olympus and the gods Chiron informs Percy he will get settled into his cabin and then more information will come to him As Chiron goes to escort Percy he reveals his true form from his wheelchair a towering centaur  Chapter  I Become Supreme Lord of the Bathroom  Chiron now in centaur form gives Percy a tour of the camp Percy learns that this was Grovers second chance as a keeper after he failed five years ago Mr D and the Council of Cloven Elders are discussing Grovers role with Percy Seeing the twelve cabins set in a U Percy realizes each cabin is patroned by one of the twelve Olympian gods Percy is lead into Cabin  by Annabeth which is the Hermes cabin for undetermined campers as well as children of Hermes Percy meets Luke Son of Hermes and cabin counselor  Percy was given his minotaur horn from Grover but keeps it to himself as a lot of the children of Hermes are eyeing it and Hermes is god of thieves Annabeth and Percy walk together Annabeth revealing that monsters like the Minotaur and the Fury or Kindly Ones do reform eventually Percy feels out of place at the camp though he has similar traits to other campers Another camper Clarisse daughter of Ares God of War drags Percy into the toilets to haze him Percy causes the toilets to explode with toilet water defeating Clarisse and her friends prompting Clarisse to declare war on Percy and Annabeth to want Percy on her team for Capture the Flag   Chapter  My Dinner Goes Up in Smoke  Percy wonders who his father is as the absent parent is the godly one Annabeth informs him he may never know as many campers do not get claimed The camp is meant to protect demigods from monsters out in the mortal world the camps borders keeping monsters out unless summoned inside the camp Annabeth explains Percy would only be allowed to leave camp if he was assigned a quest  Percy asks Annabeth about the Summer Solstice which prompts her to recall a time the camp visited Mount Olympus last Winter Solstice when she overheard something had been stolen and if it was not returned by the Summer Solstice there would be war This was when the weather began to thunder and be worrisome Percy and Annabeth return to their cabins and Percy talks with Luke Luke reveals Annabeth desperately wants a quest but was told to wait for someone special That night at dinner campers are given magical goblets which have any drink requested and campers are required to burn part of their dinner as offerings to the gods Percy begs to be given a sign about his father   Chapter  We Capture a Flag  Percy begins to discover what hes bad at and which activities he has some skill in finding some skill in sword fighting He manages to beat Luke in their first sparring which excites Luke though Percy is unable to repeat the feat Grover tells Percy that he has to successfully protect Percy during a quest to acquire his searchers license his greatest dream Grover explains that the Big Three which Percy heard from Clarisse during their argument refers to Zeus Poseidon and Hades Children of the Big Three are more dangerous and powerful than other demigods which prompted the brothers to make an agreement to no longer have children after too many of their children caused catastrophic events in mortal history WWIIZeus broke this pact by having a daughter who sacrificed herself helping other half bloods get to camp to escape monsters Zeus turned her into a tree as she was dying turning her into the tree that marks the boundary outside the camp on Half Blood Hill   During Capture the Flag Percy is on Annabeth and Lukes team and left to guard the creek border Clarisse and her friends attack Percy shocking him with an electric spear As he falls into the creek with a surge of energy Percy manages to defeat them all even snapping Clarisses spear Luke wins the game for his cabin Annabeth having set Percy up as a distraction Annabeth had been invisible nearby but reveals herself and sees Percy has healed in the creek Suddenly a hellhound from the Fields of Punishment attacks Percy but is brought down by arrows Chiron examines the creature saying someone must have summoned it in the camp Prompted by Annabeth to get in the creek to heal a green light shines over Percy a holographic trident shining over him Chiron proclaims Percy has been claimed His father is Poseidon god of the oceans Schedule Runner Up Read The Lightning Thief Percy Jackson  The Olympians by Rick Riordan I Accidentally Vaporize My Maths Teacher through We Capture a I	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased sheigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  domit persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be trying to release at least one a week starting in the new year Acheaa Dream of Divine Scams  Part I

I	Harry and his  year old wife are sat in their cramped home She decries the neighbours have  bathrooms and we have only  Its so rough waking up in a subtropical climate in the worlds sixth most affluent neighborhood and still not being able to have what other couples have  bathrooms      Harry adds All we ever wanted was to live a normal life just like everyone else But Im really worried for my childrens future The  million pound inheritance we had when we fled the UK is all we had when we arrived here All we wanted was to give our children a normal life Instead we have to explain to them why little McKaylah and little Jamison from across the street do have a yacht when we are forced to spend our holidays in the Bahamas      Megan softly weeps and dries her tears on an Hermes blanket  I just cant believe it has come to this We had so many dreams for our children and now  she gestures across the cramped  square meter living room We managed to get a few odd jobs since arriving and have managed to scrimp together  million dollars but how is one supposed to live off of that for any length of time with inflation numbers like this Harry put an arm over her shoulder and whispers sweetly My love Dont fret think about the palm trees of providence     Megan adds If I wouldve been a  white I surely wouldnt have had to put up with this nonsense Harrys face tenses Its all just so unfair he says When my brother dated my now sister in law they were given none of the special treatment Megan has been given Megan was given  staff a fulltime security detail an invite to Sandringham before we were engaged offered to accompany the Queen Square that with Kate who was chased by paparazzi whilst only a fresh grad without any support no special invitations or even security Why hasnt Megan gotten the same treatment the rest of the family has gotten      Megan composes herself and says I just know other people dont have to suffer like this Why were we dealt this hand in life Having been born into a family where theres generational trauma and favoritism uncles make bad jokes and family members sometimes even die Who else has to deal with any of that      When we first started dating we were treated like rockstars Especially when I mentioned I was mixed race   she leans in  You know they celebrated in the streets of South Africa just like they did when Mandela was freed Harry smiles We were send on a semi royal tour of the country the plebs paid for our weddings Daddy bought us a cottage and everyone was cheering us on for being a fresh wind and the type of modern couple the family needed Megan And then  She snaps her fingers  stories began to leak about how I mistreated staff Harry And how I threw a tantrum over a tiara that wasnt mine then shit really hit the fan when we belittled and insulted the British press every single time for sticking to the agreements we had made with them      Megan Well and that was the catalyst all of a sudden we realized that the public and the royals had been mistreating us from day  and we had to flee right H  She looks at Harry for confirmation whispers under her breath I call him H Harry nods and says Yes it was attrocious all of a sudden some critical notes started to appear in the newspapers I was beside myself How could I ever expect my family to live like that Should we have just NOT read the newspapers anymore Or changed our behaviour      Harry rolls up the sleeves of his tailor made shirt and plays with his  dollar Rolex watch He looks downtrodden And after everything we did for the UK as well Megan spend hundreds of thousands of my Daddys money on designer clothing Megan stares at the noses of her Aquazzura pumps and squeezes his hand Its a knife in the kidneys  Harry yells out Megan sits up and adds Remember I even wrote messages of empowerment on baas what else could I have possibly done      The pair starts making gutteral sounds when Archie interupts asking Whats for dinner his fathers face lights up briefly I dont know my love please ask ny what the chef has prepared Hes become a real foodie Megan whispers  Im just so devastated we arent able to take him to Nobu every single night All every parents ever wants for their children is to see them happy I honestly dont know how I can ever give him what he needs under these circumstances Harry poingently adds Lets not forget the sacrifises we have to make either Love Megan nods her head and adds No butler it is so challenging      Harry jumps up all of a sudden visibly irritated and gesturing at Archie Thats another thing I just cannot believe my family did not break royal protocol to make Archie a prince Why the following of the rules now When Megan was given all of these priviledges before Its the unequality I just cant live with  How will we ever tell him hes not a prince How can I possibly explain to him that his family decided to follow the law and not break it so he can get the title he I	This is not a drill  After years of continued inaction and hollow promises  is shaping to be the year that kicks off decisive regulatory action regarding sustainability across the fashion industry  France of course started the year with a bang by introducing new mandates for fashions largest brands requiring them to provide indepth information regarding material composition manufacturing location and other environmental characteristics linked to their products  The law applies to brands that sell more than  items annually in France and generate revenue above  million from domestic sales  New York and California have also passed recent bans on the toxic chemicals commonly used in waterproof outerwear The proposed New York Fashion Act which combines exacting due diligence and transparency requirements could also expose brands to penalties worth up to  percent of global revenue if passed  This flurry of regulatory action taking shape across the EU and the US is set to end years of inaction over the fashion industrys environmental and social footprint  Obviously this is great news So whats the bad news Simply put brands are not ready for these changes to take effect  Compliance with these new regulations will be challenging to measure and brands will have the devils job of uncovering how much impact production and operations genuinely have on the environment especially on a perproduct basis  While many of you may be unsympathetic toward brands in this scenario consider this quick fact A lack of readiness means brands are highly likely to delay and request grace periods as they scramble to obtain the information and establish the systems needed to document each products impact  Some proposed regulations will likely take years to pass fully Fortunately others  like Frances newest law  will require companies to act now  Regardless the risk of deteriorating ones brand image or facing potential fineslegal action has prominent brands like LVMH taking action now For example their recent partnership with the data management platform Fairly Made was established purely to gather and keep track of the information it needs to comply with these new regulations   will be an interesting and exciting year for the sustainable fashion movement to say the least  TLDR As exacting laws on transparency and ethical practices grow nearer brands are scrambling to pick up the pieces to avoid potential legal action and monetary andor reputational losses The action itself is welcome news but the true change will likely take some time to manifest as brands will need time to establish the systems and processes to comply with these newly proposed laws  xB  Read the full article here    For brands looking to boost sustainability within their eCommerce stack   Weve Got Good News and Bad News On the Wave of Regulation Poised to Rock the Fashion Industry
