I	Please discuss anything relating to FedEx GLS or ParcelForce here Anything from your experience positive or negative questions regarding delivery wait times or delivery issues and delivery damage images all belong in this megathread  xB  This decision was made on polling our community  xB  Frequently Asked Questions  xB  Who will ship my Steam Deck  xB  In North America USCA this will be FedEx RMAs are also processed by FedEx  xB  In Europe this will be GLS In the UK this will be ParcelForce or EVRI formerly known as Hermes usually in times of industrial action RMAs in Europe are by DHL  xB  In Komodo regions  we arent sure yet It will almost certainly be a large local courier service  xB  Regardless of who ships it you will receive a tracking number to follow your Decks progress  xB  Im stuck on Shipping Soon help  xB  Its normal for your order to stay on Shipping Soon for several days We usually see Steam Decks delivered within  working days after placing the order A business day is considered MonFri  xB  If it has been longer than  working days and its still on Shipping Soon you should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update in which case you should contact Steam Support  xB  My tracking says preadvice  awaiting parcel help  xB  This is a normal step in the process this means your parcel is somewhere between Valves warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do FedExGLSParcelForce deliver on Sundays  xB  FedEx delivers to  of the US population on a SundaySundaySunday  xB  In Europe as with most delivery companies GLS  ParcelForce does not typically deliver on a Sunday They may do so in times of peak demand around Christmas but outside of this its unlikely  xB  Both FedEx and GLS do deliver on Saturdays though  xB  UK My parcel is stuck in customs what do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for customs checks Depending on several events outside of the control of GLSParcelForce there are many different reasons why this could take a long period of time  xB  My Steam Deck is delayed Im annoyed  xB  Sorry to hear that your Steam Deck has been delayed Unfortunately as with any delivery service its possible for issues and delays to occur during the delivery process  xB  So long as your shipping provider is giving you frequent updates and has not elapsed more than  working days without an update hang tight  xB  If you havent received an update in over  working days MonFri please contact Steam Support  xB  My Steam Deck is brokenstolenlost from delivery help  xB  You should contact Steam Support as soon as possible so that a replacement can be arranged  xB  xB   Shipping Megathread December

I	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased sheigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  domit persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be trying to release at least one a week starting in the new year Acheaa Dream of Divine Scams  Part I

cleanser lotion  Then an herbmint facial masque which I leave on for ten minutes while I check my toenails  Then I use the Probright tooth polisher and next the Interplak tooth polisher this in surfaces  I rinse again with Cepacol I wash the facial massage off with a spearmint face scrub  In the shower I use first a wateractivated gel cleanser then a honeyalmond body scrub and on the face an exfoliating gel scrub  Vidal Sassoon shampoo is especially good at getting rid of the coating of dried perspiration salts oils airborne pollutants and dirt that can weigh down hair and flatten it to the scalp which can make you look olderThe conditioner is also good  silicone technology permits conditioning benefits without weighing down the hair which can also make you look older  On weekends or water before starting  Afterwards splash cool water on the face to remove any trace of lather You should use an aftershave lotion with little or no alcohol Never use cologne on your face since the antiaging eye balm Baume Des Yeux followed by a final moisturizing protective lotion  A scalpprogramming lotion is used after I towel my hair dry I also lightly blowdry the hair to give it body and I	In  cyber criminals used deepfake to impersonate the voice of the CEO of a German company and demand a fraudulent transfer of   to  They tricked the CEO of a UKbased energy firm  into urgently wiring said funds to a Hungarian supplier in an hour  Later that day the criminals made another call again impersonating the German CEO and asked for a second payment  He became suspicious and immediately called the authorities  Unfortunately the money that was transferred to the Hungarian bank account was already moved to a bank account in Mexico and distributed to other locations Making it harder for the authorities to trace   Several officials said that this was the first cybercrime using a voicespoofing attack in Europe Authorities are yet to determine the culprits behind the cybercrime operation  Luckily the  firm was insured by Euler Hermes Group which covered the entire cost of the payment  AIbased impersonation attacks are just the beginning of what could be major headaches for businesses and organizations in the future  Watch video     xB  cybersecurity cybermaterial infosec cyberstory europe eulerhermes ceo ai deepfakes mexico hungary Cyber criminals used AIbased voice to impersonate CEOs voice

I	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased sheigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  domit persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be trying to release at least one a week starting in the new year Acheaa Dream of Divine Scams  Part I

I	I woke up early the next morning Like really early I looked over at Roses alarm clock It was  AM  Carefully I got up and checked on Rose She was sound asleep At the very least I could feel at ease knowing she was definitely having a good dream  I snuck out into the living room Thats when I heard Mom and Martin talking  Yeah I know it isnt the most polite thing in the world I get it But when its your Mom and the man she likes who wouldnt eavesdrop  Without making a sound I crept to the edge of the hallway wall and listened in on their conversation  You should tell her the truth Martin said She deserves to know  I know that but I also know if I tell her shell be hurt  Shes a tough kid I can tell  Who were they talking about Me or Rose  But if she finds out the truth before you tell her that will upset her more Martin added  I know how to raise my child  There was silence after that  I peeked around the corner to see Martin and Mom standing across from one another near the tree Mom had her arms crossed Martin stood there with a slight frown Im sorry Victoria I know you do I wasnt trying to suggest anything else He got closer wrapping his arms around my mom gently   Mom wrapped her arms around him in return Its okay I know youre only concerned about Lupa  So it was me they were talking about  Then they kissed Im not sure why but seeing that made me feel awful It made me feel angry It was like watching Mom betray our family I could almost imagine Dad sitting up on Olympus watching this happen  I stepped out causing Martin to notice me Lupa He asked breaking from the kiss  Lupa Mom said turning to face me  There were so many things I wanted to say To yell about But everything just hurt so much I turned away and ran  Wait My mom yelled after me  I slammed into Martins door and swung it open then I turned into the hallway and booked it as fast as I could from the apartment building   After a while I ended up in Central Park on a small bridge It felt so much like back in camp when Chanel bullied me Like the entire world was ending  I sat and I cried Again I failed I wasnt able to keep the promise I made  There was no chance of our family ever being complete Dad wasnt coming home And Mom shes moved on too But Im still here  Things stayed like that for half an hour Then I heard a womans voice calling from nearby Help She yelled Please  What was going on I stood and looked to see where the yelling was coming from It seemed to come from a wooded area  I took Diligence from my pocket and slid the bolt manifesting the celestial bronze blade in my grasp I didnt know what was going on but if someone was in trouble I had to at least try to help them  As silently as I could I snuck through the woods looking for whoever was yelling for help An owl hooted nearby causing me to jump I swung toward the sound of it and saw a branch sway Guess it flew away  There didnt seem to be any sign of anyone having been here Then I heard someone whisper psst  I swung toward the sound only for another whisper to come from elsewhere Psst over here a girls voice called  Someone was messing with me Hello I whispered back shuffling toward where I thought the voice came from  Something seemed seriously off about whatever was going on This was a stupid idea I was almost going to turn around and walk away when the snare got me I shot up into the air and hit my head on the ground as I went up My sword clattered from my hands Everything was hazy far away Below me I saw two shapes exit from the shadows Both of them were laughing Look brother we caught another  I groaned at them in protest as I dangled by my foot  Shut up dummy youre gonna make a really good stew the other said He sniffed the air You smell like an Olympians brat too he bellowed in laughter They always taste better  This was really it This was the end This was how I was going to die chopped up and made into some monsters stew I ruined Christmas and now I was going to break everyones hearts by dying too  I watched the two shapes from above as they talked  Something caught the moonlight A spear skewered one monster through the chest causing it to collapse and dissolve into dust  The remaining monster looked toward where the spear had come from and bellowed in anger Coward Come out  Someone exited from the shadows a spear in one hand a shield in the other They advanced toward the monster who circled around Soon they were like two wolves in a clearing just looking for the chance to pounce on one another  You killed my brother the monster grumbled Im gonna kill you too godling  Oh relax hell be back I mean unless hes too stupid to find the way out of Tartarus the man chuckled taunting the monster His voice I know that voice But from where  The monster took the bait and rushed him With one good thrust from his spear it was over The monster dissolved into dust  Whoever it was they looked up at me then looked around the area A few seconds later they lowered me to the ground   Their face seemed familiar but I just couldnt put it to a name Youre okay here They took something from their pocket and brought it up to my mouth I tried to fight back of course but it was no use Something warm slid down my throat It tasted like smores Immediately the pain lessened Nectar  I coughed a few times as they picked me up and held me in their arms Lets go home  Despite my I	Hi rRepGirls   Business of Fashion released their Sustainability Index today and as the topic of sustainability comes up often in Rep vs Authentic debates I thought this would be interesting to the sub  Sustainable is a real buzzword right now in the same way as clean is with beauty I have numerous bones to pick with that term its thrown around a lot without much thought to what it means or the metrics you should evaluate it on Sustainability I think isnt a YesNo metric but a scale of how sustainable a brand is  BoH broke Sustainability down into  dimensions Transparency eg supply chains Emissions Water  Chemicals Materials Workers Rights and Waste  Luxury brands it discusses in order of BoHs ranking of sustainability   Kering score  which owns Gucci Yves Saint Laurent Bottega Veneta Balenciaga  PVH Corp score  which owns Tommy Hilfiger and Calvin Klein  Hermes score   LVMH score  which owns Celine Dior Fendi Givenchy Loewe Louis Vuitton Marc Jacobs  Richemont score  which owns Cartier and Chloe  Heres the full report and the main infographic for mobile users  Methodology   Methodology drafting Industry research and expert interviews inform the Index targets and metrics selected to measure progress The first draft of the methodology is devised  Sustainability Council consultations Our Sustainability Council reviews the methodology in full and partakes in consultations to refine the targets and metrics These are finalised and shared with the Council  Companies sent questionnaires Companies are notified of their inclusion in the project and are invited to complete a questionnaire of the metrics with publicly available evidence This is optional and not all companies participated  Research companies BoF researchers review each company and populate the questionnaire with evidence of relevant public disclosures to award preliminary points crosschecking and verifying evidence in responses submitted by the companies  Companies receive preliminary results and fact checks BoF researchers conduct quality assurance checks to ensure companies have been scored consistently and fairly against the metrics before sharing preliminary results with the companies along with any fact checks  Responses are reviewed Fact check responses and additional comments from the companies are reviewed and individual consultations with Council members over specific metrics take place  Data is compiled and finalised If a company provided additional information or disputed a finding this was reviewed and then either adjusted or not as considered appropriate  Final analysis and report prepared Data from each company is compiled into one complete dataset which is used to determine final scores and points of analysis BUSINESS OF FASHIONS SUSTAINABILITY INDEX AKA HOW SUSTAINABLE ARE LUXURY BRANDS REALLY

should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for or read any of these items This book may be the first time a person learns about it Please keep rbookclubs rules on spoilers and the consequences for posting spoilers in mind  Everyone has a different perception of what is a spoiler so here are a few examples of what would be spoilers   Just wait till you see what happens next   This wont be the last time you meet this character   Your prediction is correctincorrect   You will look back at this theory   Here is an Easter Egg    You dont know enough to answer that question yet   How do you firsttimereaders feel about this detail that was tagged and finally submit  Lets get to it Here are the chapter summaries  Chapter Summaries  Chapter  I Accidentally Vaporize My Maths Teacher  We begin the story with a warning from the title character Percy Jackson He urges us to close the book immediately Percy Jackson is a  year old boy who attends Yancy Academy a private school for troubled kids His life changes dramatically during a field trip to the Metropolitan Museum of Art Previous field trips did not go well for Percy at his previous schools accidents having occurred on every trip On this trip two chaperones led the group of students Mr Brunner the Latin teacher and Percys favorite and Mrs Dodds the math teacher Percys only friend Grover is on the trip as well   After a disagreement with his school bully cy Bobofit at the water fountain Percy is falsely accused of pushing her when she suddenly finds herself soaked in the ankle deep water Mrs Dodds leads Percy away from the group demanding a confession from him as she transforms into a horrid creature with bat wings and yellow fangs Mr Brunner suddenly appears and tosses Percy a ballpoint pen that turns into a bronze sword Percy swings the sword as the monster lunges at him and it turns to dust Dazed by this experience Percy finds that when he returns to the group no one remembers Mrs Dodds   Chapter  Three Old Ladies Knit the Socks of Death  No one recalls that Mrs Dodds was ever at the school or even existed which convinces Percy something else is going on Frustrated that hes the only one that seems to know Percy continues to fight with cy neglect his grades and even disrespect a teacher which gets Percy expelled from Yancey Academy Percy decides the only final he will study for is Mr Brunners Latin final and he goes to Mr Brunners office for help Percy overhears a conversation between Mr Brunner and Grover about Percy and the incident with Mrs Dodds They talk about magical mist making all of the students and teachers forget Mrs Dodds and Grover explains how Percy may be the only one who can save them before the Summer Solstice  After the school year ends Percy confronts Grover on the bus about his conversation with Mr Brunner Grover reveals his role as Percys protector The bus breaks down and as they step off the bus Grover and Percy see three old women knitting huge socks and staring at Percy As Grover makes Percy promise to walk to Percys house together one of the old women cuts a string off the socks with a pair of large shears Grover reveals thanks to Percys prodding that the cut signifies that someones going to die  Chapter  Grover Unexpectedly Loses His Trousers  After the bus stops at the terminal Percy ditches Grover and walks home on his own Before readers enter the apartment Percy describes his mother Sally museum Percy explains and they run to the call Percy realizing that Grover has hooves for feet  Chapter  My Mom Teaches Me Bullfighting  While driving away from the storm Percy sees a large creature such as virtual stadiums can be used to place  billboards or promotional materials For example the virtual concert  venue Fortnite recently hosted with Ariana Grande attracted over twenty  million unique viewers  Its a mirror image of the real world  A metaverse PR  strategy requires the brand to create a unique experience for its  audience Unlike traditional PR which relies on long press releases  metaverse audiences want to get their hands on an experience Therefore  the PR strategy should be creative and fresh For example luxury  fashion brand Balenciaga has created an exclusive virtual garment  collection for characters in the video game Fortnite The luxury brand  is known for its highend athleisure and luxe sneakers and found that  gamers were the perfect target audience  In the metaverse a brand must create exclusive partnered collections  that solve real and virtual problems This requires exploring synergies  with other brands which will keep a brand relevant in the meta world  Another effective PR strategy is brand storytelling Brands should  consider the fact that the metaverse will be a democratic space where  the user can participate in the campaign The goal of a PR strategist is  to cultivate a positive relationship with all stakeholders This  requires a strategic approach with earned owned and paid media  Its easy to apply  Metaverse PR is a very effective tool for launching a blockchain  project It can help you generate awareness for your product and brand  There are many ways you can use metaverse PR Here are a few examples  You can hire a metaverse billboard for around  a month and have it  seen by hundreds of thousands of people  The first method involves partnering with influencers This method is  perfect for blockchain projects Because metaverse was built with  blockchain at its core its users are already familiar with the  technology Thus they will understand and care about blockchain  projects  Its a strategic tool for publicists  In an age of new media brands are turning to metaverse PR  to increase brand awareness This new trend requires creative  oneofakind PR efforts Effective strategies include virtual goods  brand syndications storytelling and reputation management If done  correctly Metaverse PR can be a strategic tool for publicists to  leverage  A key component of metaverse PR is communitybuilding relations results The  goal is to build a healthy relationship with all stakeholders  Its a path to success  Brands are embracing the metaverse to reach a new audience and  increase their brands awareness Examples of brands that have done this  include Panera Bread Burger King Chipotle American Express CVS and  LeBron James Some are even filing trademarks in the virtual worlds  Brands should create a highquality website and build a strong social  media presence Keeping an active presence on the internet will help  them avoid losing opportunities and frustrations from frustrated  customers brand  To stay ahead of the competition brands need to be on top of the  latest technology and innovations Traditional marketing strategies like  influencer partnerships and social media promotion are brand  A luxury brand is a brand that is associated with highquality expensive items These items can be clothing accessories or products from a specific category such as wine  There are several factors that make a luxury brand unique For example a luxury brand typically offers more variety than other brands This means that it has more options for products and accessories Additionally a luxury brand typically has a higher price tag than other brands This means that it is more expensive to purchase one of its products  Some of the most popular luxury brands are Chanel Louis VuittonGucci Dior and Prada Why is Gucci so expensive These brands offer highquality clothing that is perfect for special occasions or for people who want to look stylish and elegant They are also popular among celebrities and other wealthy people  What is the Market  There is a growing demand for luxurious brands of clothing This demand is being fueled by the increasing cost of living and the trend of people wanting to show off their wealth There are a number of upscale brands that cater to this market including Ralph Lauren Gucci and Prada  Some of the main reasons why these brands are popular among highend consumers are their quality clothing their exclusivity and their history Ralph Lauren has been around for over  years and is known for its stylish clothes Gucci is wellknown for its luxury bags and accessories Prada has a long history as a fashion brand that appeals to both men and women  These brands are not cheap however so it is important to be able to afford them if you in  it is important to understand the trends that are currently happening in the market You can do this by reading industry publications talking to other businesses in your sector or attending industry events  Finally it is important to keep in mind that not all luxury brands are created equal Some of the most prestigious brands in the world are known for their high quality products and excellent customer service If you want to sell your products as a luxury brand you need to strive for the same level of excellence  Supply and Demand in   In  the global luxury fashion market is expected to reach a value of US trillion This means that the market will be larger than the global automobile industry and it will continue to grow at a significant rate  One of the main drivers of this growth is increasing demand from highincome consumers in developed countries These consumers are increasingly looking for designer brands that offer luxurious products at affordable prices  As a result many highend luxury brands are expanding their operations into developing countries These brands are able to offer competitive prices and highquality products because they can rely on strong demand from affluent consumers in those regions  This trend is likely to continue in  as more luxury brands move into developing countries to capture market share In light of this it is important for individuals who are interested in luxury fashion to keep track of the latest trends and developments in the market  The Global Luxury Market  The luxury fashion market is growing rapidly and there are R	   Purchasing expensive timepieces is a wise decision Premium watches are another item you can invest in that will add value to your life besides acquiring jewelry that will make you stand out from the crowd Some novice watch enthusiasts find it challenging to choose the type or design to buy because most luxury watches are identical  We will go over the several factors you should think about before purchasing a luxury watch in this articleBy doing this you can acquire a watch that you will like and one that will add to your collection In this blog we will tell you factors which you must keep in your mind while buying Jewelry  Watches of your choice   Researching about prices  Luxury timepieces can cost as much as expensive smartwatches Regarding it there is no debate They are still available at various pricing points particularly based on the collection and design For instance if you compare the prices of an Omega Seamaster and a Grand Seiko Spring Drive watch you will see that they are nearly identical Other brand collections including those from Rolex and Audemars Piguet cost a little more  Its crucial to look at the various pricing points to ensure that the watch you choose fits your budget It would help if you tried to avoid spending more than you can afford Purchasing a highend watch does not need burning a hole in your wallet   Choose highdurable materials  All of these highend timepieces are manufactured with premium components But how longlasting are they exactly It would help if you considered the materials durability and its qualities For instance would the sports watch you intend to purchase be resistant to all weather conditions  Choosing a watch made of very durable materials does not necessarily mean spending the most money Not because a precious metal watch can endure extended exposure to rain or sunlight You can look through the watchs parts to find out more about what it can do You will be able to gauge its strength in this way If you want to buy premiumquality luxury watches check Shopify alternative free sites to purchase your dream watch   Select Watch That Suits Your Style  After deciding on the brand you want to purchase it is time to pick the appropriate styleA range of watch collections with distinctive styles and aesthetics are offered by each watch brand Make a thorough comparison of each depending on your personal traits What you want to avoid doing is buying a watch that doesnt suit your lifestyle  When choosing the style keep its purpose in mind as well Choosing sports and outdoor watches is preferable if you intend to utilise them for activities However you should select something more professional if you want to wear it to work every day   Check The Size  Movement  With watches size always matters A watch that is too big or too small for your wrist could have longterm consequences If the watch is too huge it will make you feel uneasy and if it is too small it will look like a childs watch Trying them on is the key On the other hand if you purchase from an internet retailer you may check the dials size to ensure that it is the proper size   Learn The Various Movements  You should be aware of the many watch movements in addition to its visual appeal There are numerous watch movement types but only two are used in most luxury watches mechanical and quartz  A complex system of highquality parts is used to construct mechanical timepieces These components support your watchs perfect movement Quartz is utilized in analogue clocks though which are batteryoperated Automatic watches are ideal if you appreciate the fine craftsmanship and detailed detailing Quartz is a better choice though if you want a perfect timepiece with the same level of precision   Conclusion  Consider these factors before you purchase your dream watch and invest your money in it Looking for a reliable source to buy your watch Check out our website Factors To Consider While Buying Premium Watches
